The following tables show all transportable [repository objects](ABENREPOSITORY_OBJECT_GLOSRY.html) of the current system that are [released APIs](ABENRELEASED_API_GLOSRY.html) and can be used in [restricted ABAP language versions](ABENRESTRICTED_VERSION_GLOSRY.html).

Any repository object that can be used in a restricted ABAP language versions must be classified with an appropriate release contract ([C1 contract](ABENC1_CONTRACT_GLOSRY.html) in general). But not all repository objects with a release contract can be used in a restricted language version.

-   The first three columns show the repository objects or parts of repository objects.
-   Column `Release Contract` shows the [release contract](ABENRELEASE_CONTRACT_GLOSRY.html) that is used for releasing the API.
-   The two subsequent columns show, whether the API is released for restricted ABAP language version [ABAP for Cloud Development](ABENABAP_FOR_CLOUD_DEV_GLOSRY.html), [ABAP for Key Users](ABENABAP_FOR_KEY_USERS_GLOSRY.html) or for both.
-   Column `State` shows the release state that can be *Released* or *Deprecated*.
-   In case of deprecation, the successor object is shown in column `Successor` if available.

-   For more information about released APIs, refer also to the [SAP Business Accelerator Hub](https://api.sap.com/) and [SAP S/4HANA Cloud - Released objects for ATC Check](https://github.com/SAP/abap-atc-cr-cv-s4hc).
-   The class `CL_ABAP_DOCU_RELEASED_APIS` creates a similar list, where the result can be restricted to certain release contracts or language versions and also non-transportable objects can be selected.
